Yo, lets go. Here's a sampler platter  pick your flavor and we can dive deeper: ^ref-86a691ec-1-0

---

###  **Algebra**

Solve for $x$: ^ref-86a691ec-7-0
$(3x - 5)(x + 2) = 0$
 Solutions:
$x = \frac{5}{3}$ or $x = -2$

---

###  **Geometry**

Area of a circle: ^ref-86a691ec-16-0
$A = \pi r^2$
If $r = 4$:
$A = \pi \cdot 4^2 = 16\pi$

---

###  **Statistics**

Mean of: $[4, 8, 15, 16, 23, 42]$ ^ref-86a691ec-25-0
$\mu = \frac{4 + 8 + 15 + 16 + 23 + 42}{6} = \frac{108}{6} = 18$

---

###  **Calculus**

Derivative of $f(x) = x^2 \sin(x)$: ^ref-86a691ec-32-0
Use product rule:
$f'(x) = 2x \sin(x) + x^2 \cos(x)$

---

###  **Linear Algebra**

Dot product of $\vec{a} = [1, 2]$ and $\vec{b} = [3, 4]$: ^ref-86a691ec-40-0
$(1)(3) + (2)(4) = 3 + 8 = 11$

---

###  **Cool One: Eulers Identity**

${e}^{i\pi} + 1 = 0$ ^ref-86a691ec-47-0
Links:

* $e$: exponential growth ^ref-86a691ec-50-0
* $i$: imaginary unit ^ref-86a691ec-51-0
* $\pi$: circle constant ^ref-86a691ec-52-0
* 1 and 0: identity elements ^ref-86a691ec-53-0

---

Want real analysis, discrete math, probability, number theory, signal processing, or quantum field theory next? ^ref-86a691ec-57-0
